                                    6581     438.     *   VBLD uses ORVYL's VCAT module for CATALOG access methods.  So   *
                                    6582     439.     * when VCAT is called, FSBR, RQBR, and CTR should point to dummy    *

                                    6585     442.     * return.                                                           *
